Foreword
                   President of the Family Federation for World Peace and Unification  Hwang Sun Jo

 Devote Your Heart and Loyalty
You didn't want to come, but how about showing some understanding! (Laughter) People from Jeolla Province really dislike losing out. (Laughter) They really dislike losing out. Isn't that right?
 Today is not Gwangju's day but Jeonju's day. That's why when I woke up this morning, I prayed for Jeonju rather than Gwangju…. My heart is in Jeonju now. But if the person next to me keeps holding me back, what should I do? If that's the case, let's talk for just a short while, it's 25 minutes past now, let's talk for about 15 minutes, okay?
 Ah, can you all hear me? "Yes" Can I speak quietly? The speaker sound is strange, it's not good. Can you hear me here? "Yes" 
 To achieve a goal, preparation, environment, and timing are necessary
 To accomplish something great in the world, you need to have a big heart and prepare a lot for it. Without preparation, a person cannot achieve a big goal. Therefore, if the goal is big, you need big preparation for it. It requires preparation through long periods of trial and training. If the preparation is wrong, even if the time for success comes, you cannot achieve the goal.
10   
 Many heroes and martyrs have come and gone on this earth, but for them to achieve national or global accomplishments, they had to lay an environmental foundation that could be achieved. Without laying an environmental foundation, it was not possible. Also, no matter how well the environmental foundation is laid, if God does not match the timing, success is not possible. Environment, heavenly fortune, and timing are necessary. There is timing.
 Even when looking at the four seasons of spring, summer, autumn, and winter, each season has its own timing. Spring has its spring timing, summer has its summer timing, autumn has its autumn timing, and winter has its winter timing. Similarly, in serving the great heavenly providence, there must be timing.
 Therefore, what has God been doing until now? Of course, God has been working to save people, but creating the global democratic world within the Christian cultural sphere was to prepare an environmental foundation to meet a certain time at the end, the final time that God has prepared.
 When the foundation reaches a certain level, and the time that God has determined arrives, who will come? Who will come? The returning Lord, who will take on the leadership responsibility to guide all of heaven and earth, must come. That's how it is.
 Therefore, no matter how great a person is in any era, to demonstrate that greatness, there must be an environment, and that environment must be united with the person, and the person must match the timing. This applies not only to individuals but also to organizations. It applies to nations and the world. For an individual to succeed, such an environment is necessary, and the same applies to families, nations, and the world.
 Then, while family success is success and national success is success, what God ultimately desires is the success of the entire universe.
11 
God desires the ultimate success of the entire universe, so He has hoped for it and prepared the environment accordingly, and as the environment is prepared, He sets the timing to send a global Messiah to achieve the cosmic purpose. Do you understand? "Yes" That's how it is.
 The timing and environment of the Unification Church are ready, but there is no one to move
 Then, when we look at the Unification Church today, how big is its purpose? What purpose does the Unification Church have, and what is it trying to achieve? As far as I know, it has the biggest purpose in the world. And so far, it can be seen as having the most wonderful ideology. Here, not only people are moving, but the spiritual world is also infiltrating. Do you know that? The spiritual world is infiltrating. This is not just a gathering of people; the spiritual world and God are also involved. That's how it is.
 Then, to achieve this great purpose, what is needed? A foundation is needed. How big is the foundation of the Unification Church now? How big is it in Jeonnam? It's not much. However, the historical foundation prepared by God through hard work is now being inherited by us. Many religions and ideologies are like that.
 If those religions are bound by outdated traditions and do not absorb the new historical era's foundation prepared by God, they will inevitably be divided into two or three. In the end, the leaders will clash and fight…. Problems will arise. Then we can just take those who don't fight. Do you understand? Of course, this applies to religious organizations and many global ideologies and thoughts. As I look around the world, the global environment is ripe for development centered on the Unification ideology. It is ripe. And when we look at the heavenly timing, it is all set. It has passed. The time is ripe.
 Then what is the problem? Today, our Unification Church is becoming more and more of an issue nationally. The Unification Church is becoming an issue nationally. When we look at Korea, what has been done so far…. What I have been working on is how to support this nation, which does not have a traditional ideology, with the Unification ideology. Due to the merit of your hard work, it is gradually infiltrating the upper and lower classes. Isn't that right?
 And even when we look at Korea itself, the time has come. The time has come, but now the problem is that if the environment is ripe and the time has come, there must be people who can move that environment and time. When I look closely, they are all young people, young people. Their eyes are very bright, and their faces are very youthful. Can you embrace and carry this country? Huh? There are no people, no people. Although there are Unification Church members, there are not enough Unification Church members.
 Love the time and environment and devote your heart and loyalty
 
Then what should we do? How can you break through this environment and cross over? How can you break through from Korea to the world? When we look at this issue, it is a very big problem. So what is the one secret key to solving this? Huh? What is it? The environment was prepared by God, and the timing was also set by God.
 Why was it made this way? To achieve God's great purpose. To achieve the purpose, God has taken responsibility and come forward, so of course, knowledgeable people are needed externally. People with abilities are all needed, but more than that, people who can love this environment and time are needed. People who can love the time and environment are more needed. To create today's environment, how much has God worked, and how many of our ancestors have walked the path of sacrifice to make this time possible…. Loving this time and environment. Then where is the environment? It will be the foundation where you can go out and work. When is the time? It is the daily connection with God through your loyalty and devotion. This daily issue becomes a problem here.
 Then, even though you are in a position of insufficiency, knowing that human resources are lacking, should we despair here? No. The only thing needed here is to love this environment and time for God and to be loyal and sincere to God. That's all there is. Sincerity! Devoting your heart and loyalty! That's all it takes. If there is someone who devotes their heart and loyalty, for that person, no matter how prepared the time and environment are, they cannot be surpassed.
 Who becomes the owner? The person who devotes their heart and loyalty will be the owner, and only that person has the qualification to be the owner. A Ph.D. does not become the owner. If a Ph.D. comes and works, they are just a worker. They cannot be the owner. Do you understand? Huh? Do you understand what I'm saying? "Yes" The final conclusion is that knowledge is not the issue, education is not the issue, and the person's ability is not the issue. What is the issue? Devoting your heart and loyalty.
 Look at the past. A girl like Yu Gwan-sun, during the time when Japan was controlling 30 million people at will, opposed the Japanese, and at that time, she was not considered normal. However, she was loyal to the nation when the nation could not be loyal, and she devoted herself when the nation could not. Therefore, she has always held an unforgettable ideological leadership authority in our Korean nation. Isn't that right? "Yes" That's how it is.
 Although it was not the time, and the environment was not prepared, and the purpose was not achieved and failed, if there is someone who devotes their heart and loyalty when the time and environment are prepared, what will happen? Who will kill them? What will happen? If there is a child of heaven who stands up with the loyalty of those who devoted themselves when the environment was not prepared, what will happen to those children? Have you ever thought about that? What will happen to those children? The more they move, the more they will rise. The more they move…. But don't stop along the way. I was born for this, and if I work, this is the only thing. With this mindset, if you devote your heart and sincerity for one year, two years, three years, the longer you do it, the more you will rise. Do you understand what I'm saying?
 The owner who controls the environment and time is a person
 
But when I look at our young people, if they are sent to a region, for about 1 year, 2 years, 3 years, around 3 and a half years, when they have been in the Unification Church for about 3 and a half years, they are enthusiastic and excited. Most people are. Most people are enthusiastic. I mentioned it yesterday. After about 3 and a half years, when they pass the 7-year mark, they lose energy and fall out. Don't do that.
 Heroes are not separate. If you devote your heart and loyalty throughout your life with the determination you had in your youth, even if the time is not right for you to be active, that time will come. The historical fortune that the person can occupy will come. So even if they are not recognized in their time, as time passes, they will surely be recognized. This is the historical development. However, now the time has come, and the environment is prepared, so if you move, you can achieve the purpose that God desires in your time. If you think you can reach the goal, we are incredibly fortunate.
 So, I am the same. Although I am in a position to guide you, what I have to do is not to use means and methods. Nowadays, politicians are good at using means and methods. Means and methods are temporary. The issue is how to endure with patience and perseverance based on normal principles. When you meet the time and environment, don't be hasty. Since the time and environment are already prepared, if I endure for 10 years and have the loyalty to carry that environment for 10 years, the entire environment that moves for 10 years will inevitably become a great purpose because of me. God will surely make it happen. That's how it is. But if you try a little and then turn away because there are no good results…. That won't work.
 Especially, the weakness of a small nation is that. Look at the life of refugees. Refugees who kept changing their businesses couldn't develop. But those who held onto one thing and went to the end almost all established a foundation. It's the same principle.
 Therefore, the foundation that the Unification Church has built in South Korea so far, and the global fortune and the religious foundation that God has prepared through the providential course, we must all devote our heart and loyalty! Do you understand? "Yes" The standard of loyalty in this world environment is to be the highest in loyalty and devotion among any nation, any religious person, anyone.
 So, if you resolve to push forward for a hundred years, even to your grandchildren's generation, without retreating, then God's will to be fulfilled through Korea cannot be moved no matter how much it is tried. It will surely be fulfilled. Then, if it is set for God to fulfill this will in 30 years in your generation, we can shorten that 30 years to 10 years. How can that be done? By tripling the proportion of sincerity and loyalty, tripling! Triple the patience and sacrifice. It's simple. It's simple.
 When you think this way, then who is the owner who can control the environment and time that has been achieved? It is a person. Do you understand? It is a person. The extent to which a person, with united determination, can overcome the entire environment with loyalty and sincerity determines the success or failure of the goal, the length of the distance. Do you understand? "Yes" 
 Wouldn't it be nice if you could quickly restore this Republic of Korea to the Father's embrace? "Yes" Are you just going to sit and watch, huh? "Yes" You rascal! (Laughter) It's good if the neighboring village people do everything for you, and then you can just ride in a car and dance in a flashy world, why should I sweat and bleed…. Some people say, 'If believers in Jesus and religion believe to be saved, why not enjoy youth, play, drink, dance, and do everything you want, and then when you're exhausted, reluctantly believe in religion! Then just get a diploma and go to heaven.' (Laughter) Well thought out, well thought out! (Laughter) There's no such law! There's no law, so where are you going? Inevitably to hell, going to hell. When you go to hell, you wear several hats. (Laughter)
17 
 Those people are trying to use religion as a stepping stone for themselves. They are trying to use religion, heaven, and the heavenly way. So they go to hell with several severe hats. People from Jeolla Province are wise and really dislike losing out. So if they know that, they won't think that way even if you tell them to. Then what should you do? You should devote your heart and loyalty, right? Huh? Right? "Yes" 
 Be a person who is as loyal as an ox
 
Among animals, which animal is the most loyal? "It's a person" Among animals? "Dog, ox" Ox! You know well. Ox. Is it a person? People can't be loyal. This rascal just runs away at the slightest loss. The ox is loyal. This one, even its skin is sold, and its bones are all licked clean. Of course, the meat is eaten, and there's not even a drop of soup left. (Laughter) Nowadays, even the feet, they make jokbal soup, what, jokbal what soup? They even boil the tail.
 Then, if God has worked so hard to create this historical environment for the Republic of Korea and has given us this time, people like oxen who are loyal should emerge. People like oxen. People like oxen! Do you understand? "Yes" Among Abraham's altar offerings, there are three main offerings: one is a dove, one is a lamb, and what is the other? "An ox" Ox! In symbolic terms, this is the era of the ox. It's the era of the ox. God likes oxen. The era of the ox! Does He like them to eat them? God likes oxen to eat the meat, right? Isn't that so? "No" Farmers like oxen because they are bundles of future meat, right? Why do they like them? "To make them work" To work them…. To work them for food, to work them for food? (Laughter) They work them and eat them, eat and eat again.
 So God, in the end, must make people like oxen. People like oxen. Look at the ox! An ox with a shiny, plump rump never carries a load, right? Huh? An ox with a plump rump carries a load, right? "Yes" A skinny ox doesn't carry a load, right? (Laughter) Ah, the fate of this ox is doomed to ruin, that. Even if it gets fat, it has to be worked, and if it's skinny, it gets eaten, and if it's skinny and falls over, it gets eaten…. (Laughter)
 When you think about that, God, in the end, must fulfill His plan for this earth, for all of heaven and earth…. There is a plan to build the kingdom of heaven, but can God just sit and make the kingdom of heaven? Huh? "No" No. It's not possible. Then, to build the kingdom of heaven, should people be like rabbits? Can they be like rabbits, just looking for sunny spots and picking up acorns? People like oxen must emerge. Your faces look strange. 'Surely, this teacher is trying to work us like oxen…' But I'm not the one working you. (Laughter) God says it must be so, God.
 Then let's think about it. (Recording briefly interrupted) Then, if we think that we are working with the effort of an ox, in a position that sums up the whole, we are not wrong. That person is not a neighbor. That person is your Father, your Father. Our Father! When you know, it's our Father. Our Father is working so hard. Then, to become His children, what should we become? Should we become pigs? "No" Just eating…. Huh? In symbolic terms, that's what it means. Because He has devoted such loyalty and sincerity like a great ox for humanity, for His children, today we must become like calves to become His children.
19 
I'm not saying to become calves. That's what it means.
 As a sacrificial offering like an ox, let's move the environment and meet the day of liberation
 
Then, when we look at the term indemnity restoration today, in the end, the one who can overturn this heavenly fortune and time, the environment prepared by God, is what? It must be the sacrificial offering that becomes the focal point of solving the problem. Isn't that right? Abraham was made to suffer and suffer, and when the time came, he was told to offer a sacrifice. Everything depended on whether he offered the sacrifice or not, right? Moses also depended on whether he struck the rock twice or not, right? "Yes" Jesus' final prayer at the Garden of Gethsemane was also crucial, right? It's all the same. It all revolves around the standard of sacrificial offerings….
 Will this time pass or not? It doesn't just pass. Do you understand? On the foundation of devotion, in the end, it is through the standard of sacrificial offerings that it is overturned. There, a struggle of bloodshed occurs. What happens to the sacrificial offering? It is cut open and offered, right? It must die. Without experiencing the pain of death here, it cannot be resolved.
 From this perspective, today, Unification believers, on behalf of the thirty million people…. The fortune that God has prepared until now is coming to us. There is no doubt. This time is coming to us. The Unification Church is the altar of atonement for the thirty million people, and it has appeared as the sacrificial offering of atonement.
I am a church member. Do you understand? Hm? "Yes." Then, as the time of departure approaches, we come to the conclusion that we must be prepared for overall sacrifice. For this, we must be ready for a certain day.

In the process of moving forward, we must become like oxen before this nation and people... In order to save this country, we must be grateful even if we become sacrificial offerings like oxen and should not complain. Even if it takes 10 or 20 years... Do you think the seven-year course is all there is? You must be prepared to go further. Otherwise, it won't work. Loyalty and sincerity arise from that.

What will we do with loyalty and sincerity? Will we become a sword that can distinguish between the world of death and the world of life at the foremost sacrificial position for God, or not? Will we become a condition or not? Our hope is to make this judgment, and inevitably, we must cross that peak and be offered as a victorious sacrifice before heaven, so that the day of the second liberation for thirty million people can finally come. The first liberation day has come, hasn't it? Now, the ideological second liberation day must come, followed by the third liberation day, which will be the global liberation day. That is what I believe.

The second liberation day is the hardest. The second is always the hardest. In the case of Cain and Abel, the second was difficult, and Noah's son Ham, the second, was the hardest. When it comes to the God of Abraham and the God of Isaac, Isaac, the second, was difficult, so Isaac had to go out as a sacrifice. Among God's sons, Adam, the first son, failed, but Jesus, the second son, had to risk death to make a judgment. In any era, the second is the problem, the second is. The second is the problem.

Therefore, the second... Until now, external liberation has occurred, but ideological liberation has not been achieved. In Korea... Ideological unity has not been achieved. Everyone is acting separately. Therefore, what we must aim for is to bring the thirty million people into a unified ideological sphere and achieve ideological unity so that the day can come when we can sing the song of liberation. This is the most difficult task. Once this is done, the world is simple. The world is simple. The world can be moved within a few years depending on the strategy.

As we enter such a critical stage, what should you do? With loyalty and sincerity, if you move with the determination to become sacrificial offerings like oxen in this environment, then a day of ideological liberation centered on our will is sure to come. Do you understand? "Yes." Would you like to try it? If you don't, you will fail. If you don't...

Become a person with a thorough ideology who sacrifices for the people

Those who left the Unification Church are now coming back. When they left, I said, "You will surely follow me later." They looked at us and thought, "These poor people, lacking in thought and critical ability, sweating for something... For others? I'm busy eating myself, why starve for others? I hate that kind of ideology," and they ran away. But Korea is nothing special. It only gets worse and worse if it doesn't change. That's why they come back. They left stubbornly but crawl back in. (Laughter) They left like humans but come back like animals. If they are treated poorly here, they will be treated poorly.

Now, if they come back, should we hold a welcoming party for them? According to the parable of the prodigal son, should we hold a welcoming party, seat them in high positions, dress them well, and have many Unification Church members praise them with both hands? Times are different now. It's different from the past. I told them to put all those people on hold, on hold. That doesn't mean they shouldn't come. They can come, but there is one more procedure. You can come into the Unification Church freely, but you absolutely cannot leave freely! Try leaving, see what happens.

There are many people in Seoul who left our church, but there's nothing fun in the world! There's no fun, only increasing curiosity, leading to curiosity sickness. (Laughter) So those who left have nowhere to go, so they look for others who left. They all gather together and wander around. They wander around, but there's nowhere to rest! "Oh, you go. You go," they say. (Laughter) So if I were to meet them, there would be many people to meet. But I say to put it on hold. There's nowhere to go. In the future, all the young people in South Korea will come into the Unification Church. Soon, I will strengthen the organization, strengthen it. Do you understand? "Yes." Organization, unity, and practice, action! Without organization, it won't work. Until now... For that, something is needed behind the scenes, and it must be done.

Therefore, let's create people who can comply with orders, have a thorough ideology, and can sacrifice for the people like oxen. Do you want to become like oxen? "Yes." Oxen? "Yes." Oxen? "Yes." Just add "right" to oxen. That's why I say, "Right!" Ah, it's the oxen era, and I think it's the time for oxen to come. Swallow everything whole, "Right!" (Laughter) "Right!" "The ox that will come in the future," that's what it means, in the future. Korean is interesting when you look at it. "Right, right," means the ox that will come in the future! (Laughter) "Right" means the Unification Church. Do you understand? Think like that. When you hear "right" somewhere, think, "Ah, that's the Unification Church!" (Laughter) It's really true. It's not a joke. Digest it like that.

Set the standard for God to cooperate

Then what will happen? If ten such people live, that household cannot fail. Even with just three people, they can rebuild the house. Do you understand? "Yes." If all the people of a nation are like that, they will surely create a heavenly kingdom. Do you understand? "Yes."

What I am worried about inside... Look. To make South Korea a heavenly kingdom now, oh my... After traveling abroad, I thought, "Should I retreat? Should I pack my bags and go back to America and become an American citizen and work as an American? Oh, should I just stay as a Korean?" What do you think I thought? What do you think? From a worldly perspective, I definitely want to become an American. Everything is ready. Just flip the switch. Just change the direction of the plus and minus.

But look at Korea. Oh, I have to dig a hole in the ground. Do you want to dig a hole in the ground? Do you want to dig? You don't answer, so you must not like it. When will we build all this to that standard, beyond that standard... To create a heavenly kingdom on earth, oh, my bones must melt away! The bones must melt away. So there are times when I want to abandon Korea and run away. Wouldn't it be nice to run away? "No." Hm? "No." But, there must be a reason why I can't run away. Why? Because these calves are all starving and crying "Mom, mom!" (Laughter) They keep following, wanting to eat something, so it would be a big problem to abandon them. So I can't abandon them. Otherwise, there's no attachment. If you do it, I'll do it too. If you don't, I won't either.

Now, I have fulfilled my responsibilities as a teacher. Only one thing remains. If I do just one thing, even if I die, our will is to unify the world. To swallow the world. If people can't do it, the spirit world will mobilize and do it by force. "Hey, you! Will you do it or not?" They will put a spear to President Johnson's chest and say, "Will you do it or not?" Do you know that? In the future, if it's a communist, they will put a needle in Brezhnev, the communist leader, and say, "Hey, you! You don't believe in God? Taste God!" (Laughter) But the reason they can't do that is because they are not the ones who can do it. To move the leaders of a country, even a small country, there must be a decisive standard that can judge them.

Noah endured for 120 years, receiving persecution from countless people, and when he stood on the victorious foundation, the value of that victory was such that even if God judged all people, He would not feel guilty, and even if Noah's efforts were elevated to the position of glory for all people, it would not be enough. They struck with that standard set.

Similarly, for a nation or people, there is no decisive standard to judge all the leaders of each country. Do you understand? Then what do we do? How do we cooperate? They are only greedy and don't do what they should... Once a perfect plus is created, a minus automatically appears, right? "Yes." Hm? "Yes." When a perfect plus is created, a perfect minus is created by God in any way. They provide the necessary relative conditions for that perfect plus.

Women should study the Principle thoroughly

Therefore, regardless of the spirit world or the physical world, if we, centered on the Unification ideology, can completely embrace this nation with God's heart, and if only the sons and daughters who can completely embrace it are born, no one can invade them. If they invade, they will be struck. Until now, no matter how much the Unification Church was persecuted, there was no stomachache or diarrhea, right? Hm? It's strange. Usually, when people worship other spirits, problems arise, but why doesn't it happen with the Unification Church, which God loves? It's to set an absolute standard. For other spirits, it's enough to set the standard within the village, but not for us. This is higher. Until it becomes high, we endure trials and suffering to set a perfect, proud standard of value that can be boasted to the universe. That's why we have to suffer for a long time. Hm? "Yes." The more righteous a person is, the longer they suffer through historical courses. Those who can achieve great desires are those who have worked long on public matters. It's a common truth.

Then, what should the Unification Church do to save the world with a global ideology? What should we do for a long time? "We must suffer." We must suffer. So, people of Jeolla-do! Will you try it? "Yes." Will you try it? "Yes." Hm? "Yes." Then only men will do it, right? "Yes." "Women will do it too." (Laughter) Only men will do it, right? "Yes." Only men will do it! Only men will do it, right? "Yes." "No." (Laughter) Women should rest, then. (Laughter) Do you welcome it? "No." Do you welcome it or not? "We do not welcome it." Does it work just because you say you don't welcome it? We only want men to do it. Only men will do it, right? "Yes!" (Laughter) So, do you welcome it or not? "We do not welcome it." With that attitude, it won't work. You must say "We do not welcome it" loudly. So, since God is on the side of the weak, I will be on the side of women. (Laughter) Sorry, gentlemen! (Laughter) Let the women join. When I get involved, I stand with both legs. Do you understand? "Yes." You seem to like it. (Laughter)

But what mission does the teacher have? Just to build a bridge. Just to build a bridge. Once you cross it, it's your responsibility. It's not always about taking responsibility. Heaven only plays the role of building the bridge. So, will women join? "Yes." Oh! (Laughter) I feel frustrated when I see these women! But women have worked hard in the Unification Church.

Then, if men and women wrestle, men win. (Laughter) But in verbal fights, women win. (Laughter) There are strengths and weaknesses. Why are you laughing like this? There are strengths and weaknesses, right? So, what is the weapon of the Unification Church now? The words of the Unification Church, right? "Yes." It's not the power of the Unification Church, but the words. Men may struggle a bit, but if women arm themselves well, they have a lot of utility. (Laughter) It's impolite to say utility, but they are very useful. Women are good at speaking. When men say three words, women say an average of five. (Laughter) Also, in the world of men, if charming young women are armed with the Principle and come and go, even grandfathers will like it for no reason. (Laughter) Uncles will like it for no reason...

In the past, it was said that if a hen crows, the country and household will fall, but now is not such a time. Hm? Men have ruined the country, right? Hm? "Yes." Did men ruin it, or did women ruin it? "Men ruined it." (Laughter) It's seen as men who ruined it. So, this won't work. Having married a crippled man, having made the country like this, I am not crippled, so even if I wear a skirt, I will change into a suit. Do you understand?

Unification Church women can wear suits. (Laughter) And it's okay to wear pointed hats instead of round ones. (Laughter) That's what we should do. If it saves the country, that's enough. Men should follow along, and if they eat better because of women, that's good. "Haha, I got the best wife!" If they boast about their wife, that's enough. Will the household fail because of that? Women shouldn't despise their husbands, saying, "You lazy bum, just eating like a cat..." Instead, they should say, "Ah, if it weren't for my husband, I wouldn't have been able to do this..." and lead them over. That's how it should be. Isn't that right? Young brothers and sisters, you are working hard even at this time. Although I cannot dare to join you from here, with tears, with hope, with heart... This is how it should be.

Heart, circumstances, and hope! (Written on the board) Centered on God's will, the heart must be aligned, and centered on circumstances, hope must be aligned. Circumstances are life, life. Without going through circumstances, you cannot live a life in unity with Heaven. Without going through the heart, you cannot stand in a principled position. Without aligning hope, you cannot achieve the world of purpose.

Among these three, you must either align your heart and circumstances or align your heart and desire. Generally, people cannot go through circumstances. As we are going through the path of restoration now, it is not something to despair over if you cannot act. If you cannot act, you must draw hope and burn with heart, saying, "God, Your hope has not perished." I will create a foundation of life and God's circumstances for our Unification group fighting in front of the thirty million people. If there are conditions where they cannot freely act in accordance with the will, even if I cannot move, I will add strength with my heart, I will support them in all ideological standards, or if family members visit, even if I cannot go, I will hold them and cry to encourage them to go powerfully again. You must stand in such a position.

If you do not stand in such a position, you will fail. Otherwise, you must act together. If you cannot act, at least stand in a position to serve the visiting family members and add strength and hope to those who come with hope. Then, even if that person did not act, they can receive Heaven's grace. However, those who cannot stand in such a position and give disappointment and regret to those who visit are not family members.

The principle is to do all three at once, but if there are difficult circumstances that prevent you from doing so, you must do at least two. Someone else will take care of my circumstances. Pray for them with your heart and shed tears for them. When they visit, encourage them to run toward their desire with a sincere heart, making them feel the worth of their visit and the strength to say, "I will fight on your behalf." If you reject them and say, "Why did you come again?" you are not family.

Therefore, what is a family today? In a place of tears, you want to pray with family members rather than crying alone. When you are in a place of cross-bearing suffering, praying together with two people is more effective than praying alone. Where two or three gather in prayer, God has promised to fulfill it. That is the principle of creation. When there is giving and receiving, reproduction inevitably occurs. When reproduction occurs, the subject Heaven must intervene in the ideological realm of the four-position foundation.

Therefore, for family members living a life of faith on the path of the cross, loneliness and sadness may come. Whenever such tribulations come, you will inevitably long for a relative family member. Instead of being sad alone, when you visit and hold a family member and express your circumstances, they can supplement your strength and encourage you to overcome the enemy together. If you cannot stand in a position to comfort and support each other, you are not family or siblings.

Heaven's long-awaited true family must fight to the end.

From this perspective, those fighting on the front lines today are directly bearing the cross. For those who cannot, they must say to them, "Do not despair in the place of bearing the cross. A prepared time is coming for us, so endure!" How wonderful it would be if there were encouragement and support saying, "Brother, I will go" or "Sister, I am coming."

If, when Jesus was crucified, the beloved three disciples had been crucified alongside him, saying, "Lord! Endure your suffering. We will surely repay your grievance from Heaven and through our descendants," how much strength would that have given Jesus? If that had happened, instead of praying, "My God, why have you forsaken me?" he would have prayed, "My God, see these and quickly resolve the grievances of this world." If Jesus had prayed like that, it would not have taken 2,000 years to come down to today.

If Jesus had said to Heaven, "These beloved disciples have borne the cross of all mankind, have mercy on them. They are the ones who gave me strength in my path of death, who served me, forgetting their own death before Heaven. Are not the sons and daughters Heaven seeks such sons and daughters?" But Jesus was sorrowful because he could not stand in such a position.

Today, the Unification group is walking a difficult path. In the course of history, we are finally calling ourselves family. We are using the term brothers and sisters. This holy name! Even if Heaven and Earth disappear, this name must not disappear. Even if history is judged and collapses, even if this era is judged and collapses, this name and these entities must remain. Even if the evil world is cleared, the family of hope, the home of hope, and the siblings of hope must remain.

To do so, the family of hope must overcome the path of the world-historical cross. Therefore, today, we must overcome not only the personal cross but also the family, tribal, national, world, and even cosmic cross.

What did Heaven labor for by sending Jesus on the foundation of 4,000 years? It was to restore the sovereignty of a nation centered on the people of Israel and Judaism, which was Jesus' mission.

Therefore, even today, centered on this standard, we must go the shortest path to prevent the chaos of this three-thousand-ri peninsula, one people, and the Republic of Korea. If the elder brother goes, the younger brother must follow. If the younger brother wants to go, the elder brother must follow. If the parents go, the children must go. If the children go, the parents must go together. Under a shared responsibility, we must lead one family, one tribe, one nation, one world, and one cosmos.

Therefore, the mission of pioneering a greater cross lies on the path of restoration. We must know that we are walking through each stage of each era.

Today, you are young. Most of you here are young. "Now I know the will of Heaven. My body and emotions desire to experience Heaven's heart, and we long for a peaceful home, peaceful family, and peaceful siblings where we can sing of freedom and liberation on the foundation of desired happiness. Who can take away this longing heart?"

Thus, we must build one nation, one world, one Father, centered on the great Lord God and True Parents, forming one family. When True Parents rejoice from this central God, we hope that joy will spread to all Heaven and Earth. Even if we die a hundred or a thousand times, we must not forget our wish.

This is the greatest duty that humanity must resolve, the greatest path of the cross that fallen humans must walk. Even on the small path of the cross today...

Even when you are sleeping, there are brothers, sisters, or family members who are not sleeping and shedding tears with the purpose in mind. You must know that when you are full, there are family members who are hungry. Therefore, even when eating, you must have a tearful heart, and even when sleeping, you must have a tearful heart, helping them with spiritual strength and appealing with prayer to build an altar. Always keep the altar clean and ready, praying that you can be a sacrifice offered through me anytime, day or night. If you cannot bear the responsibility of action and reality, at least join in such internal preparation, fighting together, so that you can hold onto the bond of family going through the process of the cross on the path of tribulation. Otherwise, you will soon be separated from those who are fighting now, and you will become a dropout, a defeated soldier...

As a Unification Church member, what is the safest way of life, the safest step? Stand on the front line... Going against the storm, gritting your teeth and advancing step by step on the path of the cross. For those walking this path, that is the right way. That is the normal path.

Therefore, those who have not felt sorrow in that position cannot understand through explanation alone. When you shed tears in that position and cry out, "Father!" you understand the circumstances of the Father who bore the historical cross. When it becomes a regret that you could not be a filial child before the Father in that position, God says, "Yes, meeting sons and daughters who can become true filial children in such a position was my wish. Oh, so-and-so!" In that position, the names of filial children, loyal subjects, and virtuous women are determined. It is absolutely impossible in a comfortable position.

Therefore, today, whether farming or doing any work, in the workplace where you stay, even if you hold a hoe, you must plow the three-thousand-ri land as if you are overturning the world. "Please resolve our grievances! Fulfill the day of my desire!" You must go out with all your sincerity. You must become colleagues with those who go out like that, whether emotionally, circumstantially, or hopefully, standing in the position of going through the same cross path. Otherwise, you will...

We must build the true family we long for, the true children Heaven desires, and the true home. Who? With these hands and this body. God cannot do it alone. If God could do it alone, it would not have taken 6,000 years to come down. Because humans repeatedly failed...

To save this nation and this people, we must work from the very bottom.

Today, centered on the Unification Church, many have come. We must fight with the belief that we will take responsibility for this nation and people after going through the personal, family, tribal, and national courses.

When you look at this people, they have lost all confidence in the nation. Farmers have lost attachment to farming. They do not prioritize attachment to parents or children. They have lost everything. They have lost everything related to the nation, loyalty, and everything.

Moreover, they have lost interest. How will we manage this people? How will Heaven make these people interested and raise attachment to make them Heaven's people? Have you thought about that?

Farmers blame their ancestors, saying, "Why did our ancestors make us hold hoes so miserably all our lives?" But that will not do. Good is not only in cities. Good is not only in palaces. Rather, there is more evil in cities, and more evil in palaces. There is more innocent good in rural areas. Those who know good must transcend poverty and wealth. They must value lowly or humble positions more than extremely evil palaces. To protect it, they must be prepared to sacrifice their lives. Such people must exist.

But when you look at the Korean people today, there is no attachment. There is no interest. Then what will Unification Church members do? Because of such circumstances, today we are going through the three-year course and the seven-year course.

When we enter a village, what will we do? When we go to rural areas, we will hold hoes and cultivate the farmland that farmers have ignored until now. We will shed tears and plow the land with genuine devotion. We will hold and teach the children, saying it is the parents' fault for being ignorant. They were indifferent to the church, so we will... They did not think about the people and were individualistic, so they had no interest or attachment to the nation. We must cultivate this.

When a small girl or boy enters the village and stands in a position of opposition, although it may seem unjust and frustrating, it is the best position to arouse interest and create issues. Even if they oppose, they unite entirely in opposition, which means they have become interested. After some time, they realize they were wrong.

Looking at the young ones shedding tears and enduring a miserable life, even in severe hardships, they realize they worked hard for them. They realize that although they wanted to do well and acted from a righteous position, the young ones shed tears for this people, sweated for our rural areas, and endured the path of suffering, hunger, and persecution for our children. Where is the root of evil?
Living in the world, you see that there are many wrong and false things, right? There are many lies in society, many lies in the country, many lies in the world, and many lies in your family, right? And is there no falsehood in your own heart? Is there only pure, noble, and true things hidden in your heart? There are many lies there too, right? When you think about this, from a person's heart to the world, there are many lies everywhere. You can't deny that.

The root of evil is people.
Then where is the hometown where lies live? Have you thought about that? Where is the hometown of lies that has made this big world its stage and established its right to exist until now? Where is that hometown? Is it God? Is it my home? Where is it? Have you thought about where the hometown of lies is? If there's a lie, that's its hometown. Right?

Now, what makes up a family? What makes up a family? It's made up of family members. If you reverse the word for family members, it becomes a big problem. It becomes outdated. (Laughter) Family members make up a family, and what makes up a society? Families make up a society. What makes up a country? Societies make up a country. What makes up the world? Countries make up the world. In the end, what is the world, what is a country, what is a family? Ultimately, it's made up of people. Got it?

Then is the main base of evil the family? No, it's ultimately people. Got it? The root and hometown of evil are people.

Then is there more good or more evil? Speak from common sense. Is there more good or more evil? Now, when you look at yourself, is there more good or more evil? There's no need to ask, right? Isn't that common sense? There's no need to ask. Even if you ask a child, "Do you have more good or more evil?" they'll say there's more evil. It's a common answer. And older people, having lived until now, think they're that much more dirty and evil. Whether you look at society or anywhere else, evil is bound to develop. There is a lot of evil.

Then if the source of this evil is human, what does it mean that there's a lot of evil? It means there are many evil people. Got it? "Yes." If there are ten evil people, there's that much evil, if there are a hundred, there's that much evil, if there are a thousand, there's that much evil, if there are ten thousand, there's that much evil, if there are three billion, there's that much evil.

Then can we just leave this evil as it is? Would it be good to leave evil as it is? Until now, many saints and wise men, and those who have been called religious leaders, have fought against this by using terms like faith and religion, trying to figure out "How does this evil invade?" and "How do we eliminate the historical flow of this evil?" They have gone through immense hardship and effort, but they have not yet been able to eliminate the root of this evil or settle it, and they are still groaning. You must know that the struggle with this evil in the journey of life is still ongoing.

Then do you have the ability to eliminate all this evil yourselves? Do you have the ability? Look, how evil is your heart? Let's quietly unpack our hearts and think about it. Now, if there's a diamond the size of a fist and one the size of a grain of rice, where do your eyes and hands go? If your father is there and tells you to pick the small one, do you think you'll pick it? You'll cover your father's face and eyes and sneakily pick the big one. (Laughter) Right? "Yes." Is that good? If you ask a hundred people, a thousand people, they all have a hundred percent tendency to do that. Right? "Yes." Those are all useless things. That's what people are like. So, our human nature is something that can be treated as an extra. No matter how dignified or holy one appears, the core is all like that.

A truly conscientious person, a true person, is someone who can say, "The good things are yours, the bad things are mine." Have you seen such a person in the world? Have you seen such a person?

When you get married, you want to have such a husband, right? I'm mixing in some jokes. Why? Because some people are dozing off. That young soldier, is it your first time here today? The man in front, hey, is it your first time here today? "No." No? Listen well. It won't be a loss to listen.

To these young women, if you ask, "Who would you like the most handsome man in Wonju to marry?" is there a woman who would answer, "I hope he becomes my friend's husband"? If you ask, "If there's the most handsome man in Wonju, who would you want as your husband?" without a doubt, they'll say, "I want him as my husband." (Laughter) And if you ask the men, "If there's the most beautiful woman in Wonju, who would you want as your wife?" they'll say, "Is there a need to ask? I want her as my wife." Right, or not?

Now, let the women answer. Right, or not? Modest young lady, right, or not? Why are you lowering your head instead of speaking honestly? You know it's embarrassing, but where does that embarrassment start? Without a doubt, it's because "What's there to ask? It's common sense. The good things are mine." That's what it means.

Now, this is a big problem. People in the world all dislike bad things and like good things, right? "Yes." Then who becomes the owner of the good things, and who becomes the owner of the bad things? This is where the fight begins. A fight breaks out.

Then what should God think when He tries to save such a world? "Since everyone likes good things, you take the good things, and I'll take the bad things." Without thinking this way, He can't save it. If God had good things, people would all try to take them. Wouldn't they? So, what did God think to save such a world? He started thinking, "You take the good things, and I'll be the owner of the bad things." Eventually, what is that? It's the path that seeks such a way, and the path that goes that way is the land of the original home that goodness seeks, the path that goodness must go, and the content that goodness can enjoy. Got it? Therefore, God conducts His providence in the opposite direction of what humans desire. Got it? "Yes."

A true friend, then, is someone who welcomes and treats me from the opposite position of what ordinary people desire today. Ordinary people claim good things as theirs, but a true friend is someone who can say, "This is yours," for the sake of that friend. It's all the opposite. "If there's something delicious, I'll eat it," is the ordinary person's mind, but a true friend is someone who can say, "You eat the delicious thing," "Sad things are yours, good things are mine," should be the case, but a true friend is someone who can say, "Sad things are mine, good things are yours."

When I glance at my face in the mirror, I immediately see this.

Why did it become like this? When I was in Heungnam prison, the work there was truly hard labor. It was an ammonium sulfate fertilizer factory. In prison, there are no needles. There are no needles, meaning if clothes tear, you need to sew them, so you need a needle. Because it's sulfuric acid, things like cotton don't last a week. No matter how new the clothes are, after a week, they become worn. So you need a needle.

So what do you do? You make a needle. If you strip an electric wire, there's a steel wire, a steel cord. You cut that and grind it on a cement floor. To make this thing, what do you do? This steel cord is long, right? If it's like this, you grind the end. Grinding this makes the end, but the hardest part is making the hole. How do you make the needle hole, the eye of the needle? How do you make the hole to thread the thread, that's the problem.

What do you do? To tie a sack, you need a hook. If you have that hook, you put it on the rail, bend it, and hit it. Then it flattens. Once it's flattened, you use glass instead of a knife.... At that time, glass was more precious than anything. In the world, it was more precious than a saw, more precious than a knife. Once it's flattened, when you use it, it wears down. Because it's steel, just wearing it down doesn't work. You have to flip it and use it again. The problem is, once you bend it and make the hole, it's easy, but when you bend it the other way, seven or eight out of ten break. The frustration when it breaks after working so hard is indescribable. But when you make a needle through such effort, the joy is indescribable.

After making the hole, you have to straighten it. You have to make the end well. Even if you hold it with your hand like this, it turns. But it shouldn't turn. You have to hold it tight and do it like this, but you have to clamp it onto something hard. If you do it with something like a hand, it keeps slipping because it's steel. So it doesn't work well. When you do it like this, the hole opens. (Demonstrating while speaking)

Even now, I remember that time. That needle.... How much is it these days? About 10 jeon? "One jeon." I always remember the time when I devoted myself to a needle worth only one jeon. How precious was that one needle worth only one jeon? I lived with more devotion than fighting to pioneer the path of restoration. I devoted myself, thinking it shouldn't break. Jongdae, Sun, and Saem

To arrange an order like today, the person hosting should come beforehand and ask, 'Teacher, please give a talk this evening.' But when I sit here and start talking, well... It's not that I can't speak. If you look closely, it seems like this has become a precedent, and plans are made without knowing where the teacher is, but if I had been a little late this evening, it would have been a big problem.

Young people in the current world without values to believe in and follow

As you know, this training session is a university student training session, so it is significant and can be seen as a good opportunity to prepare an important key for the development of our church in the future.

It is a recognized fact that the criteria and rudder (方向舵) of a nation's rise and fall depend on young people. When you look at today's young people, especially as we enter the latter half of the 20th century, there are not many young people living with a mental foundation that can be the center of the future, who can handle the history of the past well and take responsibility for the hopes of the nation from a normal standard. Moreover, in a country like the United States, there is a strange trend called twist, and wherever they go, there are all sorts of variations. They drink and enjoy themselves in the evening, then go to the billiard hall the next day, living all sorts of lifestyles. The changing patterns are diverse, with dozens of scenes unfolding in a day's life.

That is also good. Changing according to the changing environment is good. However, because young people must become the center of hope in future society, they must have a cool-headed critical ability regarding the trends of that society and be able to set up a self-centeredness that does not lean towards any environment and handle things. It is good to face the environment from a responsible position, but it is a bit problematic to be swept away by social trends from a position that is not responsible. If a nation has such youth, it can be predicted that the future of that nation is not far off.

The Republic of Korea is no exception. A congratulatory speech would be to praise and encourage university students with good content and to tell them to do well in this aspect, but in reality...

In fact, university life is the best time to be distinguished from today's society and to be immersed in school. University students are in a period like the flower of life. It is a good period that anyone would want to seize and a valuable period. Criticizing the daily life of students in such a period, although not the majority, there are many students who are in a position where even ignorant people who know nothing worry, thinking, 'They shouldn't be like that...'

A while ago, a lady I met said that today's university students and recent graduates are like a school of goldfish. What is a school of goldfish? What is a goldfish? They are just stuck in a fish tank all day, swallowing and spitting out the water over and over again, thousands or tens of thousands of times. Eventually, there will be no water in the tank that hasn't passed through their mouths. What does this mean? If you go to a café these days, how is the air inside? It's murky, right? Many people are crammed in there, breathing in and out that air. And what else do they drink? They drink water. They are called a school of goldfish because they drink water with a gulping motion. This may sound like a funny statement, but it has some truth to it.

Passing through such places is also good. If you can discover something new about life there and acquire material necessary for your future development, and prepare a source or motive to run towards the future, that is also good. However, when you analyze all the ideological discussions, thoughts, and movements that take place in such places, they are in a position to be sanctioned and questioned by the present world. When we consider this fact, we know well that there are many students in a position that must be corrected.

Making young people who can purify the world through the Unification Church

Humans must live within a clear purpose and value system

So today, I want to briefly talk about 'Jongdae, Sun, and Saem.'

You are here now, but until yesterday, you were elsewhere. A person's life changes day by day. Of course, the standard you aim for may not change, but the living environment does. If there is a living water barrel (spring) under a waterfall, it gushes up. It's the opposite. To become spring water, you must gush up. Spring water is water too, but its path is different. The Mission to Celebrate Christmas

Luke 2:1-20

[Prayer (I)] December 25th, this day is celebrated by countless people living on earth as Christmas.

Through the many days of history that have passed, people should have wholeheartedly devoted themselves and been loyal to you, revealing your supreme and holy image so that you alone could receive honor and glory. Yet, how many paths of the cross have people left before you in the tedious course of restoration? We deeply recall that you are the Father who bears the sorrow of our ancestors who were trampled and torn in the midst of sadness, suffering, and adversity.

As we wander through these days, crossing over and over, to establish your desired day of liberation on this earth, you gathered weak groups to form the masses, embraced the persecuted nation, and led and nurtured them with promises throughout the tedious course of history. How sorrowful and unjust it is that the historical fact of sending the Messiah to save all people in Bethlehem in Judea remains only as a historical fact.

Today, as we reflect on such internal feelings, we repent once again for the sins of our ancestors who did not know the historical circumstances, and we repent once again for Israel's past failure to truly welcome this day.

Because we did not have such a day, we were driven into adversity and had no place to go, following the path of death on the cross with Jesus, and along with the path of bloodshed and martyrdom over 2,000 years of history, we once again experience the internal connection of those who cried out to heaven from the path of death. In this place where we comfort heaven above and comfort the countless ancestors who came and went on earth below, and in this present age, as representatives of the Second Israel to welcome a time of hope, we are truly grateful to be allowed to apologize for our shortcomings before heaven.

Father, today is a day when countless people hold various forms of gatherings to commemorate the birth of Jesus Christ, some holding colorful celebrations, and others calling your name to celebrate the birth of Jesus Christ. Furthermore, at this time, countless denominations and churches around the world kneel before your presence to celebrate the birth of the Messiah.

But among them, is there a form that can truly bring you joy, that can connect with the heart of heaven, that can say, "This is the path I have walked, this is what I have endured, this is what I have hoped for," and that can say, "These are the sons and daughters I wanted to meet," and gather them before you to express the historical circumstances and resolve the grievances of this era? When we think about whether there is a true nation, tribe, family, and children who can do this, we cannot help but think once again about the pitiful aspect that remains as heaven's sorrow. Although the appearance of the Israelites who were driven and chased has reached a victorious foundation on a global scale and established a democratic world, is there a true nation, tribe, family, and children who can serve as the axis to unite this world, centering on you, the source of life, and who can fulfill the role of the high priest, offering incense and worshiping before you at this time? Please help us clearly understand how much you long for such a true nation, tribe, family, and children.

On this desolate land, among this nation, you have already driven us out. You have tested us on lonely paths. You have refined us in places of sorrow. Sometimes, we have fought alongside you in environments known only to you, whether on paths of persecution, on paths of being driven, or in environments known only to you. When we think about the fact that the group that was chased and driven remains in this land today, we know that they are the group of unity.

Allow their bones to be filled with the desperate heart that cries out to you, and let their entire nervous system, through their marrow and all their limbs, be dominated by a burning heart of loyalty that can explode with earnestness for you alone. When asked if they are true sons and daughters, allow them to stand confidently before you and say, "Yes," and become such sons and daughters. We earnestly ask this before you at this time.

To do so, we must not become those who lament historical sorrow. We must become children who shed tears over the difficulties and sighs of this era. We must become those who realize that they must become sacrificial offerings, burnt offerings, to offer themselves as incense before you for the world of future hope.

Father, please remember the children of unity whom you love at this time. We know they are praying for your will on this cold day. Father, when they pray with tears, when they earnestly squeeze their hearts before you, please personally participate in that place, extend the comforting hand you once extended when I was in such a situation, and be with them with the same comfort you gave me when I was lonely. We cannot help but earnestly ask you to listen to this request.

Although their circumstances and conditions are different, they are your members, and although their circumstances and stages of life are small, they are in a position to connect with your global circumstances and stage, taking on the internal and external aspects of the heavenly warrior. Allow them to leave traces of victory wherever they go, and allow heaven to welcome them and the satanic world to retreat wherever they move. Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this.

Today is the last holy day of this year. We have reached the last Sunday of the sixth year in the seven-year course we have longed for. When we reflect on the sorrowful events of the past seven-year course, and when we recall the sorrowful stories within our hearts, we cannot help but feel sorry and inadequate before you. However, please allow the circumstances that were blocked by sorrow, loneliness, and worry not to become circumstances of resentment against the nation. When we think about the fact that these paths and circumstances are intertwined to open the path you have taken to find this nation and the world, we earnestly hope and wish that you will forgive the shortcomings of the nation and the sins committed by humanity before you.

Father, please embrace this nation and guide its direction so that not a single person falls behind and allow them to enter the realm of victory you have permitted, singing songs of victory and praise with glory and honor before you. Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this.

Please be with the countless congregations and children of yours in this land who are celebrating this day, and we earnestly ask you to be with the many religious people who are still on the path of the way of truth, enduring hardships to walk the path of the way.

Because heaven's grievances are bound on this earth, we earnestly hope and wish that this time becomes a new opportunity to make a promise to win in the upcoming seven-year course, along with the joy of this day, even for the countless spirits in the spirit world who long for liberation.

Now, in this one hour, allow us, who are inadequate, to spend this day within the permission you have given, and to pledge our own internal awareness to welcome the new year, and to swear and resolve before you. We earnestly ask for this.

We know that many of your children are scattered around the world, praying toward this place. Although they are separated by regions and environments, please allow their hearts to be united, and at the standard where they can connect with you, let them be united so that they can fulfill their mission as pioneers and warriors in the restoration of the universe, without getting tired. Father, we earnestly ask you to hold them and lead them to the garden of victory we hope for.

We earnestly ask that all of this be combined to praise your glory, and we offer all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

Even though they might have heard, not a single person sought to find and serve the Messiah. When we see this fact, we cannot deny that while their hearts were earnest, they neglected to prepare the foundation they needed in their actual lives. Despite observing this environment, God, because the promised time had come, could not help but send the Messiah to save the earthly Israel. Therefore, God sent the Messiah to this earth at the right time. Consequently, if Mary and Joseph had truly embraced in their hearts all the facts the angel taught them in a dream, and if they had deeply experienced and felt in their lives that the son to be born was the Savior who could save Israel and the Messiah for all people, they should have followed the testimony of the Eastern Magi, as stated in the Bible. However, although Mary remembered the birth of Jesus in her heart, Joseph was in a position of not knowing about it. Seeing this fact, we must reconsider that even the parents, who received the heavenly command and bore the direct mission, could not assume the proper stance of parents before the heavenly standard.

Mary and Joseph, who were full-term and did not know when the birth would come, should have prepared for it. If they were to go to Bethlehem, they could have sent someone ahead to prepare an inn. However, without any preparation, they went to Bethlehem, and because all the inns were full due to the many people who came for the census, they had nowhere to go and ended up spending the night in a stable, where Jesus was born. Seeing this, we can say that Joseph's family did not fulfill the responsibility of welcoming the heavenly prince, the only begotten son, with the heart that heaven desired. Mary was like that, Joseph was like that, and the relatives in that environment were also like that.

Jesus, who was ignored by family, church, society, and nation

The birth of Jesus was not only a joy for the couple in the family. It was an event that the entire tribe should celebrate. However, they could not do so. When we realize that they were not prepared, we cannot deny the fact that the parents did not fulfill their responsibility before the wish that heaven desired. If there is anyone among you who is here for the first time and doubts, saying, "Ah, I can't believe it," then pray about it, whether it is so or not.

Jesus, as the Son of God, came to this earth from the womb... His mother Mary lived for ten months with worries and pain, with concerns she could not share with others, from the time she conceived until she gave birth. It is sad that during this period, he could not live comfortably in an environment where heaven and earth could welcome him with joy. Moreover, it was also a sad thing from heaven's perspective that Mary herself could not show externally, through sincere devotion and testimony to all people, the fact that she was preparing for this event. We must think about this again.

Because it was like this in Joseph's family, the Jewish believers and the people of Israel had no choice but to be even more so. Nevertheless, since Jesus was the one who came bearing the mission of heaven and earth, it was not a matter of what environment he was born into. Until he could fulfill the purpose of God's providence under God's protection, he had to prepare for the purpose heaven had determined, even if he faced all sorts of sorrow and adversity.

Jesus began to grow after being born in this way. Even as he grew, Jesus was still a stepson to Joseph. Joseph, who heard the angel's command in a dream not to fear bringing Mary, who was pregnant, took her in a daze, but as time went by, he could not help but have human thoughts. Therefore, he could not treat Jesus from the position of the father who was sent along with heaven's promise, but rather from a position of concern in heaven's eyes.

From the time his younger siblings were born, Jesus could not help but feel the sorrow of being a stepson even more. As he grew up with many siblings, he could not place his heart in the family. This was because his father was like that, and so were the siblings who were growing up. He just silently continued to assist in the livelihood of Joseph's family, playing the role of a carpenter's assistant, only cooperating in life, without being able to present his own wishes or the great mission that was his heavenly destiny before his parents. We must know that this was the Jesus who could not stand in such a position.

Even his siblings hated Jesus. It is recorded in the Gospel of John that they criticized him, asking why he did not go up to Jerusalem if he wanted to show himself. Seeing this, we cannot deny the fact that even his siblings did not treat him as the Messiah sent by heaven.

Moreover, on such festive days, or on good days for the family, they should have allowed Jesus to be the center of joy. However, they could not create such a position centered on Jesus, and this sorrow remained as a regret for Jesus. We must know this. As he grew up, testified to the will, and set out to carry out heaven's mission, we must trace the path he walked for over three years until the end, and recall that Jesus lived in an environment where he could not establish the hope of creating a kingdom of peace on this earth, from his family, environment, church, society, or nation.

Jesus came to restore what was lost due to Adam's fall

In commemorating the day Jesus was born today, it is not only the birth that is joyful, but we must clearly understand the purpose for which he was born. He did not come on his own, but was sent by heaven, and he did not come and go as an individual, but came for heaven above and for the people of Israel below. Therefore, there was a responsibility to heaven, a responsibility to the people, and furthermore, a responsibility to the world and humanity. It was not just a limited responsibility of that era, but he bore the historical responsibility for future generations as well. We must clearly understand how lonely and difficult Jesus' life was. Then, from this emotional standard, we must long for him, become his side, and have the earnest heart to become the brother he missed, the sister he missed, the parents he missed, or the relative, uncle, or cousin he missed, and comfort him in place of the tribal environment he longed for, and resolve the unresolved regrets. We must have such a heart to welcome this day, which is what heaven and the believers who have come and gone throughout history demand.

Therefore, the moment Jesus was born was an indescribably joyful moment for God. It was a joyful moment not only for God but also for Jesus himself. It was also a moment that the people of Israel should have rejoiced in. However, the joy of heaven, the joy of Jesus, and the joy of Israel were all separated.

The joy of heaven was lost due to the fall, and in the process of pioneering the path of restoration, God became a God who walked a sorrowful path with Israel. God's joy has not been manifested until now. Since the day of the fall, there have been countless nations and peoples, but none that could please God.

Moreover, even with the ancestors who came to represent the will of the providence of restoration, God could not truly rejoice. From Abel to Noah, Abraham, Isaac, Jacob, then through the people of Israel and Moses to the time of Jesus, in that historical process, heaven could not truly have a day of joy. Although they went through the path of struggle to welcome a day of joy, they could not have a single day of joy.

If there was finally a day in history when God could rejoice, it was the day Jesus was born. The day Jesus was born was a day of joy for God. Because God rejoiced, the heavenly world rejoiced, and because the heavenly world rejoiced, all the people who stayed in the world of morality that revered heaven should have rejoiced. Jesus was born to welcome such a day. Because God rejoiced at Jesus' birth, it was a day when the child could rejoice because the Father rejoiced.

The day when Jesus fulfilled the will and God could rejoice was not only for Jesus. The purpose of selecting Israel and forming the people of Israel and establishing the nation of Israel from the satanic world was to make the day of Jesus' birth a national day of joy. Therefore, the purpose had to be fulfilled on the day Jesus was born.

In other words, it was not only Adam himself that was lost due to human fall. God's wish to communicate with Adam, God's joy that was to be achieved through Adam, all of this was shattered. Therefore, God's wish in sending Jesus was to recreate and restore what was lost due to Adam's mistake through Jesus. Therefore, the birth of Jesus heralds the birth of the nation of Israel. Along with that, it heralds a day when God can rejoice. The issue of whether the nation of Israel would emerge as a victorious nation and whether the people of Israel would welcome a day of joy with God was raised from the day Jesus was born.

Was the environment such that God could rejoice at Jesus' birth?

Today, although there are countless nations and peoples on earth, they have not yet appeared in a form that God can rejoice in from a tribal or national standard. Jesus came to connect this. Therefore, because Jesus rejoiced, heaven rejoiced, and because Jesus rejoiced, the nation of Israel could rejoice. This standard was to be achieved through Jesus' birth, but did God truly rejoice on that day? Did Jesus truly rejoice on that day? Did the nation of Israel truly rejoice on that day? When we think about this, neither God could rejoice, nor could Jesus rejoice, nor could the nation of Israel rejoice.

Because of this, the day when God should rejoice is still remaining, the day when Jesus should rejoice is still remaining, and the day when the nation of Israel should rejoice is still remaining. Therefore, to find the day when God should rejoice, the day when Jesus should rejoice, and the day when the nation of Israel should rejoice, this day is announced again and extended. The announced day is the end. To proclaim this end and carry out the movement to re-create and re-organize the lost Israel is the history of the creation of the Second Israel centered on the New Testament gospel after Jesus came and went.

Because the First Israel was lost on a national foundation, the Second Israel is organized on a global foundation. Thus, now we have reached a time when we have prepared a global foundation that can become the end. Therefore, in history, a day must come when God can rejoice, a day must come when Jesus can rejoice, and a day must come when the ideological nation of Israel can rejoice. Although Israel should have had a day when the three were united and could rejoice when they welcomed Jesus, because they did not have it, the day of the Second Coming is to make them welcome that day on a global scale. We must know that this is the day of the Second Coming.

The moment Jesus was born was a sorrowful moment for God

Today, when we look back at the nation of Israel at that time, because the social environment and the environment in which Jesus was born did not align with the will God hoped for, God's sorrow was extended. When we think about this, for us who welcome such a day, we must analyze the sorrow of the historical age once again and be able to prepare the conditions and circumstances ourselves to prepare for the coming day. Father! When we consider the three thousand li peninsula, when we look at the countless people who do not know where this nation should go, when we look at the young people wandering on the streets, we know well that it is the mission of the Unification Church to help them determine their path, to pioneer a foundation where they can live, and to show it practically. We have sworn to fight with tears for this, and we have resolved to offer our blood to comfort the Father.

As we send off the year 1966, a year full of sorrow, and welcome this new seven-year course, Father, please allow victory to dwell in it, and let all the stories of tears and blood we have shed become conditions that can relieve the Father's heart, and let all the earnest connections of loyalty we have established become the foundation of the victorious flag that can liberate and serve the Father in the world of freedom.

In front of the children gathered here today, from the womb era to the growing life course, through the ideological era, we have realized that our mission remains to resolve the grievances of Jesus and the stories buried in heaven and earth. Now, centering on such a heart, when we reflect on the past, thinking about what we have done before the Father, and clearly defining our position, please allow us to become children who can re-examine and rebuild all areas of our life and living before the Father.

Before the seven-year course tilts, please allow each of us to fulfill the responsibility of reconnecting all the lost stories to heaven and receiving public recognition from the Father in the remaining year, Father, we earnestly ask and wish.

If there are lonely children scattered in the provinces, looking at the teacher here and shedding tears, Father, please bless them. If there are those who pledge loyalty before heaven following the heart that heaven worries about, Father who loved me, please love them, and Father who protected me, please protect them, we earnestly ask and wish.

Although we have different bloodlines, we have connected the bloodline through your heart, and as family members who are not family, as brothers who are not brothers, we have been established within the ideological realm of a large family that can directly serve the Father, please deeply observe and protect us, Father, we earnestly ask and wish.

Knowing that there are children scattered around the world who are praying with longing while looking at the East at this time, we earnestly ask that you be with them wherever they go, wherever they stay.

Please allow the banner of unification to fly high and become a world sign that can herald victory for the liberation and resolution of grievances for humanity for eternity.

Please thicken the bonds of life over this entire day, allowing your stories to intertwine with our hearts and life stages, we earnestly ask.

We earnestly ask for the glory, mercy, and love of ten thousand years to be with us forever, as we offer all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen. *
